CREATE TABLE Transactions (transaction_id INT PRIMARY KEY, account_id INT, transaction_type VARCHAR(50), amount DECIMAL(10, 2), transaction_date TIMESTAMP, FOREIGN KEY (account_id) REFERENCES Accounts(account_id));</t><s>SELECT Customers.first_name, Accounts.balance FROM Customers INNER JOIN Accounts ON Customers.customer_id = Accounts.customer_id;</s>
